The Review Concierge business model is timely and effective--and it works! We have been paying tremendous attention to our online reviews for years, even being very proactive by asking our most happy patients to review us online and even providing them with a direct on-line link.  However, you just can't help the fact that one unhappy patient is more vocal than 100 happy patients. Unhappy patients will go to the far ends of the earth to disparage your practice, while the happiest get on with their lives and tend to provide no useful feedback.  The folks at Review Concierge understand these relationships and understand how to manage them to your benefit. This is especially helpful when review sights such as "Yelp" would must rather use negative information (they PREFER negative reviews). <rate>4<//rate>< Text>
Came here with some friends after running the Cloverdale half marathon, boy is it a beautiful property.  The parking situation is a bit strange, they don't have any designated spaces except on handicap space.  So you either have to park along side the driveway or do what most people do and back in between the vines.  The tasting experience here was very pleasant, thankfully our friends are club members so we were able to relax down by the pool.
The staff made it feel more like a hangout than a proper tasting which was really nice.  We were able to just take our time and enjoy the wine, the property, and the company.  The wines were all pretty enjoyable, but were a bit too light for my taste.  We didn't end up purchasing any bottles this time, but would consider buying some in the future.  One of the strangest things to me was that to join the wine club didn't offer any discounts on the wine.  It was more like they are trying to sell a membership to their property instead of focusing on the wine.  Definitely would be worth joining if you are a local, or within an hour or so.  But, for someone like me who enjoys buying and aging wine it didn't seem like a good sell.<//Text>

I love this gym!! Its large, clean and it seems that only people serious about working out come here. I have not run into anyone that is creepy or disrespectful. <Rate>5<//Rate>< Text>
One of the few places I go to where I can eat away my desires of one of the best food joints in Stockton. The atomosphere inside of this eatery, how may I explain it without being too bland. The interior doesn't matter, what matters is the aroma that hits you when you reach near the door, a overwhelming sensations strikes your stomach with a blow. The staff are nice and may be a bit stiff but it's Stockton what can I say. The establishment may be in a small area where crime is lingering but the chances of having a bad time will be low.

The prices may differ in many people, but the quantity of how much you're receiving is outstanding. Having a mix of the BBQ platter for 10 dollars with how much you're receiving sets you full for an entire day. They of course have chicken, pork platters as well almost if not the same price. Their menu has a lot to choose from and if you'd like a variety then this is the place to go if visiting. Whenever I get the chance for some pleasure food I'd usually come here.

Just a small tip. They do, do doordash, but I would rather drive there for a take out. Delivery fee comes out to 4.99-5.99 with one mix platter or a platter your order comes out to 20 dollars already. Don't get it delivered, expand and meet others going to the restaurant you won't regret it.</Text>

<userid>112433538265405983103<//userid>< review>
This place is not open terribly late, which makes coming here to enjoy the delicious offerings all the more precious. Everything is reasonably priced, the serving portions are generous for the meals, and the sides are healthy portions. But if you're a creep like me and the Loco Moco is delicious but you could do without the meat, you can order the rice, the mac salad, and the delectable gravy itself, all separately to combine yourself. You can even order a single egg if you want, cooked how you like it. The ability here to custom order is incredible. The saimin-a noodle dish with meat of your choice and green onions- is beyond tasty, and a personal favorite of mine. The chicken Katsu here (a fried chicken dish) is clearly their most popular order. Choose from a diverse menu with large enough print so you won't have to squint. They're always playing relaxing Hawaiian/reggae style music here, and it's always got an atmostphere of peace despite how busy it can sometimes get. Come on over!< /review>
